Here is the fully implemented `gui.py` file along with necessary modifications to other files:

```python
gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the graphical user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk

class GUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Add GUI elements here (buttons, input fields, etc.)
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.root, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.root)
        self.username_entry.pack()

        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.root, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.root, show="*")
        self.password_entry.pack()

        self.login_button = tk.Button(self.root, text="Login", command=self.login)
        self.login_button.pack()

    def login(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        # Call the login method from LinkedInAutomation class
        linkedin_automation.login(username, password)

    def run(self):
        self.root.mainloop()
```

Additionally, I will make modifications to the `main.py` file to include the instantiation of the `LinkedInAutomation` class and the `Logging` class:

```python
main.py
```python
'''
Main file to run the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
from gui import GUI
from linkedin_automation import LinkedInAutomation
from logging import Logging

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Initialize the GUI
    gui = GUI()
    
    # Initialize the LinkedInAutomation class
    linkedin_automation = LinkedInAutomation()
    
    # Initialize the Logging class
    logger = Logging()
    
    gui.run()
```

'''
GUI file to create the graphical user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk

class GUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Add GUI elements here (buttons, input fields, etc.)
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.root, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.root)
        self.username_entry.pack()

        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.root, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.root, show="*")
        self.password_entry.pack()

        self.login_button = tk.Button(self.root, text="Login", command=self.login)
        self.login_button.pack()

    def login(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        # Call the login method from LinkedInAutomation class
        linkedin_automation.login(username, password)

    def run(self):
        self.root.mainloop()
```

'''
Error handling file to manage errors during LinkedIn automation.
'''
class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    
    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            
            # Handle specific error cases
            if "CAPTCHA" in str(error):
                linkedin_automation.handle_captcha_challenge()
            else:
                # Handle other types of errors
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            # Log any exceptions during error handling
            logger.log_activity(f"Error handling failed: {e}")
```

'''

from logging import Logging

class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logging()

    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            # Handle specific error cases
            if "CAPTCHA" in str(error):
                self.handle_captcha_challenge()
            else:
                # Handle other types of errors
                self.logger.log_activity("Handling non-CAPTCHA error.")
        except Exception as e:
            # Log any exceptions during error handling
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error handling failed: {e}")

    def handle_captcha_challenge(self):
        # Logic to handle CAPTCHA challenges
        self.logger.log_activity("Handling CAPTCHA challenge.")
        # Implement CAPTCHA solving logic here

```python
'''
Error handling file to manage errors during LinkedIn automation.
'''
from logging import Logging
class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logging()
    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")

### gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox

class GUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()

        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()

        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()

        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()

    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            # Here you would call the LinkedInAutomation login method
            # linkedin_automation.login(username, password)
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")

    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

'''

from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright

class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration

    def login(self, username, password):
        with sync_playwright() as p:
            browser = p.chromium.launch()
            context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
            page = context.new_page()
            page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
            page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
            page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
            page.click("button[type='submit']")
            # Add error handling and logging here
            context.close()
            browser.close()

    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        # Simulate realistic user interactions

        # Manage CAPTCHA challenges
        pass

    def close_session(self):
        # Close the user session
        pass

class ErrorHandling:

    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic

            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            # Handle specific error cases

from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright

class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration

    def login(self, username, password):
        with sync_playwright() as p:
            browser = p.chromium.launch()
            context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
            page = context.new_page()
            page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
            page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
            page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
            page.click("button[type='submit']")
            # Add error handling and logging here
            context.close()
            browser.close()

        # Simulate realistic user interactions

        # Manage CAPTCHA challenges
        pass

        # Close the user session

gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
class GUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()
    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            # Here you would call the LinkedInAutomation login method
            # linkedin_automation.login(username, password)
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")
    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

linkedin_automation.py
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
    def login(self, username, password):
        with sync_playwright() as p:
            browser = p.chromium.launch()
            context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
            page = context.new_page()
            page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
            page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
            page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
            page.click("button[type='submit']")
            # Add error handling and logging here
            context.close()
            browser.close()
    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        # Simulate realistic user interactions
        pass
    def handle_captcha_challenge(self):
        # Manage CAPTCHA challenges
        pass
    def close_session(self):
        # Close the user session
        pass
```

error_handling.py
```python
'''
Error handling file to manage errors during LinkedIn automation.
'''
from logging import Logging
class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logging()
    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            # Handle specific error cases
            if "CAPTCHA" in str(error):
                self.handle_captcha_challenge()
            else:
                # Handle other types of errors
                self.logger.log_activity("Handling non-CAPTCHA error.")
        except Exception as e:
            # Log any exceptions during error handling
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error handling failed: {e}")
    def handle_captcha_challenge(self):
        # Logic to handle CAPTCHA challenges
        self.logger.log_activity("Handling CAPTCHA challenge.")
        # Implement CAPTCHA solving logic here
```

### logging.py
```python
'''
Logging file to log activities during LinkedIn automation.
'''
import logging

logging.basicConfig(filename='automation.log', level=logging.INFO)

class Logging:
    def __init__(self):
        pass

    def log_activity(self, message):
        logging.info(message)

    def log_warning(self, message):
        logging.warning(message)

    def log_error(self, message):
        logging.error(message)

    def log_debug(self, message):
        logging.debug(message)
```

This implementation includes the necessary logging methods to log activities, warnings, errors, and debug messages, ensuring that the LinkedIn automation tool can effectively track its operations and handle issues as they arise.

```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
class GUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()
    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            # Here you would call the LinkedInAutomation login method
            # linkedin_automation.login(username, password)
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")
    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()

linkedin_automation.py
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
    def login(self, username, password):
        with sync_playwright() as p:
            browser = p.chromium.launch()
            context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
            page = context.new_page()
            page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
            page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
            page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
            page.click("button[type='submit']")
            # Add error handling and logging here
            context.close()
            browser.close()
    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        # Simulate realistic user interactions
        pass
    def handle_captcha_challenge(self):
        # Manage CAPTCHA challenges
        pass
    def close_session(self):
        # Close the user session
        pass
```

**gui.py**
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from linkedin_automation import LinkedInAutomation

class GUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()
        self.linkedin_automation = LinkedInAutomation()  # Initialize LinkedInAutomation here

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()

    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            self.linkedin_automation.login(username, password)  # Call the login method
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")

    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

**linkedin_automation.py**
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
from logging import Logging

class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = Logging()  # Initialize logging

    def login(self, username, password):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")

    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        # Simulate realistic user interactions
        pass

    def handle_captcha_challenge(self):
        # Manage CAPTCHA challenges
        pass

    def close_session(self):
        # Close the user session
        pass
```

```python
'''
Main file to run the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
from gui import GUI
from linkedin_automation import LinkedInAutomation
from logging import Logging
from error_handling import ErrorHandling
if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Initialize the GUI
    gui = GUI()
    # Initialize the LinkedInAutomation class
    linkedin_automation = LinkedInAutomation()

    # Initialize the ErrorHandling class
    error_handler = ErrorHandling()

gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from linkedin_automation import LinkedInAutomation
class GUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()
        self.linkedin_automation = LinkedInAutomation()  # Initialize LinkedInAutomation here
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()
    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            self.linkedin_automation.login(username, password)  # Call the login method
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")
    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

linkedin_automation.py
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
from logging import Logging
class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = Logging()  # Initialize logging
    def login(self, username, password):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")
    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        # Simulate realistic user interactions
        pass
    def handle_captcha_challenge(self):
        # Manage CAPTCHA challenges
        pass
    def close_session(self):
        # Close the user session
        pass
```

'''
Error handling file to manage errors during LinkedIn automation.
'''
from logging import Logging
class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logging()
    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            # Handle specific error cases
            if "CAPTCHA" in str(error):
                self.handle_captcha_challenge()
            else:
                # Handle other types of errors
                self.logger.log_activity("Handling non-CAPTCHA error.")
        except Exception as e:
            # Log any exceptions during error handling
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error handling failed: {e}")
    def handle_captcha_challenge(self):
        # Logic to handle CAPTCHA challenges
        self.logger.log_activity("Handling CAPTCHA challenge.")
        # Implement CAPTCHA solving logic here

logging.py
```python
'''
Logging file to log activities during LinkedIn automation.
'''
import logging
logging.basicConfig(filename='automation.log', level=logging.INFO)
class Logging:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    def log_activity(self, message):
        logging.info(message)
    def log_warning(self, message):
        logging.warning(message)
    def log_error(self, message):
        logging.error(message)
    def log_debug(self, message):
        logging.debug(message)

    def __init__(self):

                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")

gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from linkedin_automation import LinkedInAutomation
class GUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()
        self.linkedin_automation = LinkedInAutomation()  # Initialize LinkedInAutomation here
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()
    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            self.linkedin_automation.login(username, password)  # Call the login method
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")
    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

linkedin_automation.py
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
from logging import Logging
class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = Logging()  # Initialize logging
    def login(self, username, password):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")
    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        # Simulate realistic user interactions
        pass
    def handle_captcha_challenge(self):
        # Manage CAPTCHA challenges
        pass
    def close_session(self):
        # Close the user session
        pass
```

from logging import Logging
class ErrorHandling:

import logging
logging.basicConfig(filename='automation.log', level=logging.INFO)
class Logging:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    def log_activity(self, message):
        logging.info(message)
    def log_warning(self, message):
        logging.warning(message)
    def log_error(self, message):
        logging.error(message)
    def log_debug(self, message):

'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
from logging import Logging

class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = Logging()  # Initialize logging

    def login(self, username, password):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")

    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement realistic user interactions here
                self.logger.log_activity("Simulating user interactions.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"User interaction simulation failed: {e}")

    def handle_captcha_challenge(self):
        # Manage CAPTCHA challenges
        self.logger.log_activity("Handling CAPTCHA challenge.")
        # Implement CAPTCHA solving logic here

    def close_session(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement closing session logic here
                self.logger.log_activity("Closing user session.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Session closing failed: {e}")

class LinkedInAutomation:

        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = Logging()  # Initialize logging

                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()

    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        try:

                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set

    # Initialize the GUI

gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from linkedin_automation import LinkedInAutomation
class GUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()
        self.linkedin_automation = LinkedInAutomation()  # Initialize LinkedInAutomation here
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()
    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            self.linkedin_automation.login(username, password)  # Call the login method
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")
    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

linkedin_automation.py
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
from logging import Logging
class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = Logging()  # Initialize logging
    def login(self, username, password):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")
    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement realistic user interactions here
                self.logger.log_activity("Simulating user interactions.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"User interaction simulation failed: {e}")
    def handle_captcha_challenge(self):
        # Manage CAPTCHA challenges
        self.logger.log_activity("Handling CAPTCHA challenge.")
        # Implement CAPTCHA solving logic here
    def close_session(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement closing session logic here
                self.logger.log_activity("Closing user session.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Session closing failed: {e}")
```

error_handling.py
```python
'''
Error handling file to manage errors during LinkedIn automation.
'''
from logging import Logging
class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logging()
    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            # Handle specific error cases
            if "CAPTCHA" in str(error):
                self.handle_captcha_challenge()
            else:
                # Handle other types of errors
                self.logger.log_activity("Handling non-CAPTCHA error.")
        except Exception as e:
            # Log any exceptions during error handling
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error handling failed: {e}")
    def handle_captcha_challenge(self):
        # Logic to handle CAPTCHA challenges
        self.logger.log_activity("Handling CAPTCHA challenge.")
        # Implement CAPTCHA solving logic here
```

logging.py
```python
'''
Logging file to log activities during LinkedIn automation.
'''
import logging
logging.basicConfig(filename='automation.log', level=logging.INFO)
class Logging:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    def log_activity(self, message):
        logging.info(message)
    def log_warning(self, message):
        logging.warning(message)
    def log_error(self, message):
        logging.error(message)
    def log_debug(self, message):
        logging.debug(message)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from linkedin_automation import LinkedInAutomation
class GUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()
        self.linkedin_automation = LinkedInAutomation()  # Initialize LinkedInAutomation here
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()
    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            self.linkedin_automation.login(username, password)  # Call the login method
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")
    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

linkedin_automation.py
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
from logging import Logging
class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = Logging()  # Initialize logging
    def login(self, username, password):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")
    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement realistic user interactions here
                self.logger.log_activity("Simulating user interactions.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"User interaction simulation failed: {e}")
    def handle_captcha_challenge(self):
        # Manage CAPTCHA challenges
        self.logger.log_activity("Handling CAPTCHA challenge.")
        # Implement CAPTCHA solving logic here
    def close_session(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement closing session logic here
                self.logger.log_activity("Closing user session.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Session closing failed: {e}")
```

'''

from logging import Logging
class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logging()
    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            # Handle specific error cases
            if "CAPTCHA" in str(error):

            else:
                # Handle other types of errors
                self.logger.log_activity("Handling non-CAPTCHA error.")

        # Logic to handle CAPTCHA challenges

'''
Error handling file to manage errors during LinkedIn automation.
'''
from logging import Logging
from captcha_handler import handle_captcha_challenge

class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logging()

    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            # Handle specific error cases
            if "CAPTCHA" in str(error):
                handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Use the utility function
            else:
                # Handle other types of errors
                self.logger.log_activity("Handling non-CAPTCHA error.")
        except Exception as e:
            # Log any exceptions during error handling
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error handling failed: {e}")

                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)

            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")

gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from linkedin_automation import LinkedInAutomation
class GUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()
        self.linkedin_automation = LinkedInAutomation()  # Initialize LinkedInAutomation here
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()
    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            self.linkedin_automation.login(username, password)  # Call the login method
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")
    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

linkedin_automation.py
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
from logging import Logging
from captcha_handler import handle_captcha_challenge
class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = Logging()  # Initialize logging
    def login(self, username, password):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")
            handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Handle CAPTCHA if it occurs
    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement realistic user interactions here
                self.logger.log_activity("Simulating user interactions.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"User interaction simulation failed: {e}")
    def close_session(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement closing session logic here
                self.logger.log_activity("Closing user session.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Session closing failed: {e}")
```

error_handling.py
```python
'''
Error handling file to manage errors during LinkedIn automation.
'''
from logging import Logging
from captcha_handler import handle_captcha_challenge
class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logging()
    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            # Handle specific error cases
            if "CAPTCHA" in str(error):
                handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Use the utility function
            else:
                # Handle other types of errors
                self.logger.log_activity("Handling non-CAPTCHA error.")
        except Exception as e:
            # Log any exceptions during error handling
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error handling failed: {e}")

'''
Logging file to log activities during LinkedIn automation.
'''
import logging
logging.basicConfig(filename='automation.log', level=logging.INFO)
class Logging:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    def log_activity(self, message):
        logging.info(message)
    def log_warning(self, message):
        logging.warning(message)
    def log_error(self, message):
        logging.error(message)
    def log_debug(self, message):
        logging.debug(message)

gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from linkedin_automation import LinkedInAutomation
class GUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()
        self.linkedin_automation = LinkedInAutomation()  # Initialize LinkedInAutomation here
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()
    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            self.linkedin_automation.login(username, password)  # Call the login method
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")
    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

linkedin_automation.py
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
from logging import Logging
from captcha_handler import handle_captcha_challenge
class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.proxy = None  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = Logging()  # Initialize logging
    def login(self, username, password):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")
            handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Handle CAPTCHA if it occurs
    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement realistic user interactions here
                self.logger.log_activity("Simulating user interactions.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"User interaction simulation failed: {e}")
    def close_session(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement closing session logic here
                self.logger.log_activity("Closing user session.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Session closing failed: {e}")
```

'''

from logging import Logging
from captcha_handler import handle_captcha_challenge
class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logging()
    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            # Handle specific error cases
            if "CAPTCHA" in str(error):
                handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Use the utility function
            else:
                # Handle other types of errors
                self.logger.log_activity("Handling non-CAPTCHA error.")
        except Exception as e:
            # Log any exceptions during error handling
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error handling failed: {e}")

'''
Main file to run the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
from gui import GUI
from linkedin_automation import LinkedInAutomation
from logging import Logging
from error_handling import ErrorHandling

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Initialize the Logging class
    logger = Logging()
    # Initialize the ErrorHandling class
    error_handler = ErrorHandling()
    # Initialize the LinkedInAutomation class
    linkedin_automation = LinkedInAutomation()
    # Initialize the GUI
    gui = GUI(linkedin_automation, logger)  # Pass dependencies to GUI
    gui.run()

gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox

class GUI:
    def __init__(self, linkedin_automation, logger):
        self.linkedin_automation = linkedin_automation  # Store LinkedInAutomation instance
        self.logger = logger  # Store logger instance
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()

    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            self.linkedin_automation.login(username, password)  # Call the login method
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")

    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, linkedin_automation, logger):
        self.linkedin_automation = linkedin_automation  # Store LinkedInAutomation instance
        self.logger = logger  # Store logger instance
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()
    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            self.linkedin_automation.login(username, password)  # Call the login method
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")
    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

linkedin_automation.py
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
from logging import Logging
from captcha_handler import handle_captcha_challenge
class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self, proxy=None):
        self.proxy = proxy  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = Logging()  # Initialize logging
    def login(self, username, password):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")
            handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Handle CAPTCHA if it occurs
    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement realistic user interactions here
                self.logger.log_activity("Simulating user interactions.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"User interaction simulation failed: {e}")
    def close_session(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement closing session logic here
                self.logger.log_activity("Closing user session.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Session closing failed: {e}")
```

error_handling.py
```python
'''
Error handling file to manage errors during LinkedIn automation.
'''
from logging import Logging
from captcha_handler import handle_captcha_challenge
class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logging()
    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            # Handle specific error cases
            if "CAPTCHA" in str(error):
                handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Use the utility function
            else:
                # Handle other types of errors
                self.logger.log_activity("Handling non-CAPTCHA error.")
        except Exception as e:
            # Log any exceptions during error handling
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error handling failed: {e}")
```

logging.py
```python
'''
Logging file to log activities during LinkedIn automation.
'''
import logging
logging.basicConfig(filename='automation.log', level=logging.INFO)
class Logging:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    def log_activity(self, message):
        logging.info(message)
    def log_warning(self, message):
        logging.warning(message)
    def log_error(self, message):
        logging.error(message)
    def log_debug(self, message):
        logging.debug(message)

def simulate_user_interaction(self):
    try:
        with sync_playwright() as p:
            browser = p.chromium.launch()
            context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
            page = context.new_page()
            page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/feed/")
            # Simulate actions like scrolling, clicking, etc.
            self.logger.log_activity("Simulating user interactions.")
            # Example: Scroll down the feed
            page.mouse.wheel(0, 1000)  # Scroll down
            context.close()
            browser.close()
    except Exception as e:
        self.logger.log_error(f"User interaction simulation failed: {e}")

gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, linkedin_automation, logger):
        self.linkedin_automation = linkedin_automation  # Store LinkedInAutomation instance
        self.logger = logger  # Store logger instance
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()
    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            self.linkedin_automation.login(username, password)  # Call the login method
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")
    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

linkedin_automation.py
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
from logging import Logging
from captcha_handler import handle_captcha_challenge
class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self, proxy=None):
        self.proxy = proxy  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = Logging()  # Initialize logging
    def login(self, username, password):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")
            handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Handle CAPTCHA if it occurs
    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement realistic user interactions here
                self.logger.log_activity("Simulating user interactions.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"User interaction simulation failed: {e}")
    def close_session(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement closing session logic here
                self.logger.log_activity("Closing user session.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Session closing failed: {e}")
```

error_handling.py
```python
'''
Error handling file to manage errors during LinkedIn automation.
'''
from logging import Logging
from captcha_handler import handle_captcha_challenge
class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logging()
    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            # Handle specific error cases
            if "CAPTCHA" in str(error):
                handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Use the utility function
            else:
                # Handle other types of errors
                self.logger.log_activity("Handling non-CAPTCHA error.")
        except Exception as e:
            # Log any exceptions during error handling
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error handling failed: {e}")
```

logging.py
```python
'''
Logging file to log activities during LinkedIn automation.
'''
import logging
logging.basicConfig(filename='automation.log', level=logging.INFO)
class Logging:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    def log_activity(self, message):
        logging.info(message)
    def log_warning(self, message):
        logging.warning(message)
    def log_error(self, message):
        logging.error(message)
    def log_debug(self, message):
        logging.debug(message)
```

linkedin_automation.py
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
from logging import Logging
from captcha_handler import handle_captcha_challenge

class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self, logger, proxy=None):
        self.proxy = proxy  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = logger  # Initialize logging

    def login(self, username, password):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                
                # Check for CAPTCHA challenge
                if "challenge" in page.url:
                    self.logger.log_activity("CAPTCHA challenge detected.")
                    handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Handle CAPTCHA if it occurs

                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")
            handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Handle CAPTCHA if it occurs

    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement realistic user interactions here
                self.logger.log_activity("Simulating user interactions.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"User interaction simulation failed: {e}")

    def close_session(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement closing session logic here
                self.logger.log_activity("Closing user session.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Session closing failed: {e}")
```

'''
Main file to run the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
from gui import GUI
from linkedin_automation import LinkedInAutomation
from logging import Logging
from error_handling import ErrorHandling
if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Initialize the Logging class
    logger = Logging()
    # Initialize the ErrorHandling class
    error_handler = ErrorHandling()
    # Initialize the LinkedInAutomation class
    linkedin_automation = LinkedInAutomation(logger)  # Pass logger to LinkedInAutomation
    # Initialize the GUI
    gui = GUI(linkedin_automation, logger)  # Pass dependencies to GUI
    gui.run()

gui.py
```python
'''
GUI file to create the user interface for the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, linkedin_automation, logger):
        self.linkedin_automation = linkedin_automation  # Store LinkedInAutomation instance
        self.logger = logger  # Store logger instance
        self.window = tk.Tk()
        self.window.title("LinkedIn Automation Tool")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Username Label and Entry
        self.username_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Username:")
        self.username_label.pack()
        self.username_entry = tk.Entry(self.window)
        self.username_entry.pack()
        # Password Label and Entry
        self.password_label = tk.Label(self.window, text="Password:")
        self.password_label.pack()
        self.password_entry = tk.Entry(self.window, show='*')
        self.password_entry.pack()
        # Start Button
        self.start_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Start Automation", command=self.start_automation)
        self.start_button.pack()
        # Quit Button
        self.quit_button = tk.Button(self.window, text="Quit", command=self.window.quit)
        self.quit_button.pack()
    def start_automation(self):
        username = self.username_entry.get()
        password = self.password_entry.get()
        if username and password:
            self.linkedin_automation.login(username, password)  # Call the login method
            messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Automation started for user: " + username)
        else:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Please enter both username and password.")
    def run(self):
        self.window.mainloop()
```

linkedin_automation.py
```python
'''
LinkedIn automation file to interact with LinkedIn using Playwright.
'''
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright
from logging import Logging
from captcha_handler import handle_captcha_challenge
class LinkedInAutomation:
    def __init__(self, logger, proxy=None):
        self.proxy = proxy  # Placeholder for proxy configuration
        self.logger = logger  # Initialize logging
    def login(self, username, password):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                page.goto("https://www.linkedin.com/login")
                page.fill("input[name='session_key']", username)
                page.fill("input[name='session_password']", password)
                page.click("button[type='submit']")
                self.logger.log_activity(f"User {username} logged in.")
                # Check for CAPTCHA challenge
                if "challenge" in page.url:
                    self.logger.log_activity("CAPTCHA challenge detected.")
                    handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Handle CAPTCHA if it occurs
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Login failed: {e}")
            handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Handle CAPTCHA if it occurs
    def simulate_user_interaction(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement realistic user interactions here
                self.logger.log_activity("Simulating user interactions.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"User interaction simulation failed: {e}")
    def close_session(self):
        try:
            with sync_playwright() as p:
                browser = p.chromium.launch()
                context = browser.new_context(proxy={"server": self.proxy})  # Use proxy if set
                page = context.new_page()
                # Implement closing session logic here
                self.logger.log_activity("Closing user session.")
                context.close()
                browser.close()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.log_error(f"Session closing failed: {e}")
```

error_handling.py
```python
'''
Error handling file to manage errors during LinkedIn automation.
'''
from logging import Logging
from captcha_handler import handle_captcha_challenge
class ErrorHandling:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logging()
    def handle_error(self, error):
        # Implement error handling logic
        try:
            # Log the error message
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error occurred: {error}")
            # Handle specific error cases
            if "CAPTCHA" in str(error):
                handle_captcha_challenge(self.logger)  # Use the utility function
            else:
                # Handle other types of errors
                self.logger.log_activity("Handling non-CAPTCHA error.")
        except Exception as e:
            # Log any exceptions during error handling
            self.logger.log_activity(f"Error handling failed: {e}")
```

logging.py
```python
'''
Logging file to log activities during LinkedIn automation.
'''
import logging
logging.basicConfig(filename='automation.log', level=logging.INFO)
class Logging:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    def log_activity(self, message):
        logging.info(message)
    def log_warning(self, message):
        logging.warning(message)
    def log_error(self, message):
        logging.error(message)
    def log_debug(self, message):
        logging.debug(message)

'''
Main file to run the LinkedIn automation tool.
'''
from gui import GUI
from linkedin_automation import LinkedInAutomation
from logging import Logging
from error_handling import ErrorHandling

    # Initialize the Logging class
